## <a name="windows-server-2003-r2"></a><span data-ttu-id="79868-951">Windows Server 2003 R2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79868-951">Windows Server 2003 R2</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="79868-952">Attributs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79868-952">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2003-r2-attributes)

## <a name="windows-server-2012"></a><span data-ttu-id="79868-2004">Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79868-2004">Windows Server 2012</span></span>

-   [<span data-ttu-id="79868-2005">Attributs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="79868-2005">Attributes</span></span>](#windows-server-2012-attributes)
